           <div class="text-wrapper">
            <h2 class="title">
             <a href="https://impressio.dir.bg/interview/pianistat-na-tangra-dani-ganchev-sbogom-kosyo-blagodarya-za-priyatelstvoto-i-rokendrola" title='Пианистът на "Тангра" Дани Ганчев: Сбогом, Косьо! Благодаря за приятелството и рокендрола!'>

              <strong>
               Дани Ганчев:

        <div class="topic-img-wrapper">

        </div>
        <div class="text-container">
         <h2>
          ТЕМА
         </h2>
         <h3>
          Ваксинация
         </h3>
         <p>
          Масовото ваксиниране ли е начинът да се избавим от коронавирусната пандемия? Въпреки противоречията по въпроса, това е единственият изход, който се вижда на хоризонта. Засега.
         </p>

          <h2 class="title">
           <a class="img-wrapper" href="https://dnes.dir.bg/obshtestvo/shefat-na-rzi-sofiya-pri-takav-priem-v-bolnitsite-do-nyakolko-dni-lechebnata-mrezha-shte-e-v-kolaps" title="Шефът на РЗИ-София: Ако приемът на болни продължи, до дни лечебната мрежа ще е в колапс">

            <strong>
             приемът на болни
            </strong>

            <strong>
             лечебната мрежа ще е в колапс
            </strong>
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="description">

          </p>

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
            var selectedValue = $('.sites option:selected').val();
            var $siteSection = $('#site-' + selectedValue);

            if (selectedValue !== '') {
                $siteSection.show(); // show the section that we need on change
                $siteSection.find('.sections').attr('name', 'selected_section'); // change the section name on change (prevents overwrite on selects)
            }

            $('select[name="section"]').prop('disabled', true); // disable selects that we don't need on submit

            $('.sites').on('change', function () {
                var selectedValue = $('.sites option:selected').val(); // on change get the selected value
                var $siteSection = $('#site-' + selectedValue);

                $('.sections').hide(); // hide all sections on change

                $siteSection.show(); // show the section that we need on change

                $siteSection.find('.sections').attr('name', 'selected_section'); // change the section name on change (prevents overwrite on selects)

                $('select[name="selected_section"]').prop('disabled', false); // enable the selected section ot get the right value of selected item
            });
        });
  </script>

  <script>
   var didScroll;
var lastScrollTop = 0;
var delta = 175;
var bannerHeight = $('#scroll-banner').outerHeight();

$(window).scroll(function(event){
    didScroll = true;
});

setInterval(function() {
    if (didScroll) {
        hasScrolled();
        didScroll = false;
    }
}, 250);

function hasScrolled() {
    var st = $(this).scrollTop();
    
    if(Math.abs(lastScrollTop - st) <= delta)
        return;
    if (st > lastScrollTop && st > bannerHeight){
        // Scroll Down
        $('#scroll-banner').removeClass('nav-down-banner').addClass('nav-up-banner');
    } else {
        // Scroll Up
        if(st + $(window).height() < $(document).height()) {
            $('#scroll-banner').removeClass('nav-up-banner').addClass('nav-down-banner');
        }
    }
    
    lastScrollTop = st;
}
  </script>
  <script>
   function isInViewport(node) {
  var rect = node.getBoundingClientRect()
  return (
    (rect.height > 0 || rect.width > 0) &&
    rect.bottom >= 0 &&
    rect.right >= 0 &&
    rect.top <= (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight) &&
    rect.left <= (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth)
  )
}

$(window).scroll(function() {
  var scrolled = $(window).scrollTop()
  $('.paralax').each(function(index, element) {
    var initY = $(this).offset().top
    var height = $(this).height()
    var endY  = initY + $(this).height()

    // Check if the element is in the viewport.
    var visible = isInViewport(this)
    if(visible) {
      var diff = scrolled - initY
      var ratio = Math.round((diff / height) * 100)
      $(this).css('background-position','center ' + parseInt(+(ratio * 2.5)) + 'px')
    }
  })
})
  </script>
